INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [t].[UserId] = [u].[Id]

    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Amount], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsVerified], [p].[Notes], [p].[PaymentDate], [p].[PaymentMethod], [p].[ReceiptImagePath], [p].[ReceiptNumber], [p].[ReferenceNumber], [p].[SolarRequestId], [p].[Status], [p].[UTRNumber], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UpdatedBy], [p].[UserId], [p].[VerifiedAt], [p].[VerifiedBy]
    FROM [Payments] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[SolarRequestId]
ORDER BY [t].[CreatedAt] DESC, [t].[Id], [u].[Id]

    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[AadharNumber], [s].[Address], [s].[AdminNotes], [s].[AlternateMobile], [s].[ApplicantName], [s].[ApprovalStatus], [s].[City], [s].[ConnectionType], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedBy], [s].[CurrentStage], [s].[Email], [s].[ExternalProductId], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[KVCapacity], [s].[LightBillNumber], [s].[LightBillOwnerType], [s].[LightBillPath], [s].[LightBillRelationName], [s].[LightBillRelationProofPath], [s].[MobileNumber], [s].[PANNumber], [s].[PinCode], [s].[PlanAmount], [s].[PmSuryaApplicationNo], [s].[PmSuryaLoanOption], [s].[RejectionReason], [s].[RequestNumber], [s].[RequestType], [s].[SelectedPlan], [s].[SolarProjectId], [s].[State], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[UpdatedBy], [s].[UserId]

    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ORDER BY [s].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Amount], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsVerified], [p].[Notes], [p].[PaymentDate], [p].[PaymentMethod], [p].[ReceiptImagePath], [p].[ReceiptNumber], [p].[ReferenceNumber], [p].[SolarRequestId], [p].[Status], [p].[UTRNumber], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UpdatedBy], [p].[UserId], [p].[VerifiedAt], [p].[VerifiedBy]
    FROM [Payments] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[SolarRequestId]

FROM (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[AadharNumber], [s].[Address], [s].[AdminNotes], [s].[AlternateMobile], [s].[ApplicantName], [s].[ApprovalStatus], [s].[City], [s].[ConnectionType], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedBy], [s].[CurrentStage], [s].[Email], [s].[ExternalProductId], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[KVCapacity], [s].[LightBillNumber], [s].[LightBillOwnerType], [s].[LightBillPath], [s].[LightBillRelationName], [s].[LightBillRelationProofPath], [s].[MobileNumber], [s].[PANNumber], [s].[PinCode], [s].[PlanAmount], [s].[PmSuryaApplicationNo], [s].[PmSuryaLoanOption], [s].[RejectionReason], [s].[RequestNumber], [s].[RequestType], [s].[SelectedPlan], [s].[SolarProjectId], [s].[State], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[UpdatedBy], [s].[UserId]
    FROM [SolarRequests] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ORDER BY [s].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [t].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Amount], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsVerified], [p].[Notes], [p].[PaymentDate], [p].[PaymentMethod], [p].[ReceiptImagePath], [p].[ReceiptNumber], [p].[ReferenceNumber], [p].[SolarRequestId], [p].[Status], [p].[UTRNumber], [p].[UpdatedAt], [p].[UpdatedBy], [p].[UserId], [p].[VerifiedAt], [p].[VerifiedBy]
    FROM [Payments] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[SolarRequestId]
ORDER BY [t].[CreatedAt] DESC, [t].[Id], [u].[Id]
